<div class="wp-block-uagb-advanced-heading uagb-block-41b88079"><h1 class="uagb-heading-text">Uncover the Best PM Tools with our<br>Top 25 Recommendations</h1></div>



<div class="wp-block-uagb-image uagb-block-dffac5de wp-block-uagb-image--layout-default wp-block-uagb-image--effect-static wp-block-uagb-image--align-none uag-blocks-common-selector" style="--z-index-desktop:1;;--z-index-tablet:undefined;;--z-index-mobile:undefined;"><figure class="wp-block-uagb-image__figure"><a class="" href="https://projectmanagers.net/best-project-management-software/" target="" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" srcset="https://projectmanagers.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/Homepage-big-banner-top-25.jpg ,https://projectmanagers.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/Homepage-big-banner-top-25.jpg 780w, https://projectmanagers.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/Homepage-big-banner-top-25.jpg 360w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 480px) 150px" src="https://projectmanagers.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/Homepage-big-banner-top-25.jpg" alt="" class="uag-image-16963" width="540" height="360" title="" loading="lazy" role="img"/></a></figure></div>



<div class="wp-block-uagb-buttons uagb-buttons__outer-wrap uagb-btn__default-btn uagb-btn-tablet__default-btn uagb-btn-mobile__default-btn uagb-block-29041478"><div class="uagb-buttons__wrap uagb-buttons-layout-wrap ">
<div class="wp-block-uagb-buttons-child uagb-buttons__outer-wrap uagb-block-7cedc469 wp-block-button"><div class="uagb-button__wrapper"><a class="uagb-buttons-repeater wp-block-button__link" aria-label="" href="https://projectmanagers.net/best-project-management-software/" rel="follow noopener" target="_self" role="button"><div class="uagb-button__link">Discover the best pm software in 2026</div></a></div></div>

<div class="wp-block-uagb-container uagb-block-42c13cc3 alignfull uagb-is-root-container"><div class="uagb-container-inner-blocks-wrap">
<div class="wp-block-uagb-container uagb-block-1a7d172b">
<div class="wp-block-uagb-container uagb-block-bf6db4a8">
<div class="wp-block-uagb-advanced-heading uagb-block-5e780a83"><h6 class="uagb-heading-text">Free note-taking for YouTube</h6></div>



<div class="wp-block-uagb-advanced-heading uagb-block-7a3fe1e5"><h2 class="uagb-heading-text">YNotes &#8211; My Free YouTube<br>Notes Organizer</h2></div>



<p>YNotes is a web application designed to help users efficiently organize and manage notes taken while watching YouTube videos. </p>



<p>It combines video playback with a rich text editor, allowing users to create timestamped annotations, save their work, and easily revisit important moments in videos.</p>



<div class="wp-block-uagb-buttons uagb-buttons__outer-wrap uagb-btn__default-btn uagb-btn-tablet__default-btn uagb-btn-mobile__default-btn uagb-block-7227de1d"><div class="uagb-buttons__wrap uagb-buttons-layout-wrap ">
<div class="wp-block-uagb-buttons-child uagb-buttons__outer-wrap uagb-block-524a7f6d wp-block-button"><div class="uagb-button__wrapper"><a class="uagb-buttons-repeater wp-block-button__link" aria-label="" href="https://projectmanagers.net/ynotes/" rel="follow noopener" target="_self" role="button"><div class="uagb-button__link">LEARN MORE</div></a></div></div>
</div></div>
